     data-hd-film="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/7416665508290871116/636x382_JPG-HD_7416665508290871116.jpg"
     data-hd-frame-width="636"
     data-hd-frame-height="262"
     data-hd-frame-count="61"
     data-hd-fps="7" />

  </a>
  <div class="articletext">
    <div >
      <p>
        
        Furious passengers lashed out at police, were thrown to the floor and arrested during chaotic scenes at Fort Lauderdale-Hollywood International Airport. Several people were arrested during ugly confrontations with law enforcement when 11 flights were grounded and 26 were delayed at the Florida hub on Monday night. The group of passengers who clashed with cops were angry because the last-minute disruption meant they would miss a graduation ceremony. Irate customers began beating the counters and screaming at staff, prompting security to step in in a bid to calm the situation. Shocking footage shows people shouting as they are dragged from the terminal building by police. Women were also captured attacking officers, only to be thrown on the floor. The disrupted flights are said to be over ongoing negotiations between Spirit Airlines and the Airline Pilots Association. 
      </p>
    </div>

                          <div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-large cleared" data-original-title="Comey 'wrong' to say Huma forwarded classified emails">
  <meta itemprop="position" content="2" />
  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-4486876/Comey-wrong-say-Huma-forwarded-classified-emails.html" >FBI director James Comey 'exaggerated the number of Clinton emails top aide Huma Abedin forwarded to her husband Anthony Weiner's laptop during his sworn Senate testimony'</a>
  </h2>
  <a href="/news/article-4486876/Comey-wrong-say-Huma-forwarded-classified-emails.html">
            <img  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/08/401ED30A00000578-0-image-m-6_1494314409366.jpg" height="503" width="308" alt="Comey 'wrong' to say Huma forwarded classified emails" />
        <noscript>
    
        <img  src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/08/401ED30A00000578-0-image-m-6_1494314409366.jpg" height="503" width="308" alt="Comey 'wrong' to say Huma forwarded classified emails" />
    
        </noscript>
    
  </a>
  <div class="articletext-holder">
    <p>
      
      FBI Director James Comey erred last week (pictured top during the hearing) when he falsely claimed in testimony before Congress that top Hillary Clinton (bottom right) aide Huma Abedin forwarded classified emails to the laptop of her husband, Anthony Weiner (pictured together bottom left), it has been claimed. The FBI chief told the Senate Judiciary Committee that Abedin had made ‘a regular practice’ of forwarding ‘hundreds and thousands’ of Clinton-related emails to Weiner, ‘some of which contain classified information.’ But FBI officials have privately acknowledged that Comey’s testimony was false and are now trying to figure out how to correct the record, according to the report by ProPublica.
    </p>

        <a href="/news/article-4488118/Teen-turns-throwing-woman-68-pool.html">

        <p>
            
            These are the 18 Penn State students who have been charged following the death of 19-year-old Timothy Piazza. The group of young men, who were all brothers of the Beta Theta Pi fraternity, are facing charges that range from involuntary manslaughter and aggravated assault to reckless endangerment and tampering with evidence (top row l to r: Luke Visser, Ryan Foster, .Gary Dibileo, Joseph Ems, Brendan Young, Daniel Casey. Middle l to r: Michael Bonatucci, Parker Yochim, Ryan McCann, Jonah Neumann, Joe Sala and Nick Kubera. Bottom l to r: Craig Heimer, Lucas Rockwell, Lars Kenyon, Ed Gilmartin, Braxton Becker, Michael Schiavone)
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

                <img  src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/02/401DA86000000578-0-image-a-57_1494292988993.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Inside look at Disney World's new Pandora-World of Avatar" />
            
                </noscript>
            
        </a>
        <div >
        <p>
            
            Disney World's new Pandora-World of Avatar land (inset) opens in Florida in late May at Walt Disney World's Animal Kingdom and cost $500 million to build. The enormous blue Na'vi aliens from the 'Avatar' (bottom left) movie appear sparingly, really just on Flight of Passage and a second attraction called Na'vi River Journey. There is 12 acres of land at the exhibit featuring vast concrete rock islands (top right) and manmade illuminating forest filled with detailed hand-made plants and creatures (top right). Disney also is testing out a new way to order food at Pandora. Before going to the park, visitors can pull up a menu on the My Disney Experience mobile app, order lunch and go about visiting the park (bottom right). 
        </p>

  </h2>

    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview
     src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"

Putin was personally taking the salute at the parade involving 10,000 troops and 114 units of military equipment including a Yars RS-24 intercontinental ballistic missile system (bottom right), as well as Buk-M2 (left) and S-400 Triumf (top right) missile systems. However plans to send 72 aircraft overhead were defeated by the weather - despite the Kremlin spending £1.3 million to spike the clouds with a chemical cocktail to supposedly guarantee sunshine. The fly-past was grounded because of low cloud, thwarting Putin's bid to showcase his air force and honour Russian pilots who have served in Syria.

    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview
     src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"
     data-src="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/2286923694139064366/636x382_JPG-SINGLE_2286923694139064366.jpg"
     width="636"

     data-video="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/2286923694139064366/636x382_MP4_2286923694139064366.mp4"

     data-frame-width="308"
     data-frame-height="172"
     data-frame-count="35"
     data-fps="7"
     data-hd-film="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/2286923694139064366/636x382_JPG-HD_2286923694139064366.jpg"

  <div class="articletext">
    <div >
     <p>
       
       Qantas chief executive Alan Joyce (left), who had a pie shoved in his face by an elderly man at the Hyatt Regency in Perth on Tuesday (centre), has claimed the incident was 'not unusual' considering his job. Mr Joyce had just begun speaking at a business breakfast when an anonymous man (RIGHT) walked up to him and hit him with what appears to be a lemon meringue pie (pictured). He addressed the incident afterwards, claiming he was not altogether surprised by the sudden attack. 'When you've been the CEO of an airline for nine years, there's a lot of things that have happened over that period of time, this is different, but it's not unusual. It is an unusual event, but things like this have happened in the past,' he said. In video footage of the incident (centre), the elderly man walked up behind Mr Joyce and rested a hand on his shoulder before pushing the pie into his face and rubbing it in. The airline boss took it relatively well, exclaiming 'f***ing heck' before jovially telling the audience: 'I don't know what that was about.'
     </p>

    <p>

                <div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="48" />
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/femail/article-4486656/Can-tell-face-2-000-worth-make-on.html" >Can you tell which face has $2,000 worth of make up on? Beauty guru creates two similar looks - one with 24 luxury items and the other using cheap everyday cosmetics</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/femail/article-4486656/Can-tell-face-2-000-worth-make-on.html">
                    <img  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/04/401D9B8400000578-0-image-a-3_1494300453252.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Can you tell which face has $2,000 worth of make up on?" />
                <noscript>
            
                <img  src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/04/401D9B8400000578-0-image-a-3_1494300453252.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Can you tell which face has $2,000 worth of make up on?" />
            
                </noscript>
            
        </a>
        <div >
        <p>
            
            With stars like Kylie Jenner and Kim Kardashian sporting flawless beauty looks and promoting high-end products on their social media channels, women feel pressure to splash the cash. But does a higher price tag always mean higher quality? One beauty blogger from Queensland decided to find out - by beautifying herself with an eye-watering $2,000 (£1,135) worth of 24 high-end luxury cosmetics and then comparing it to a much cheaper beauty look using around only $177 (£100) worth of 14 drug store products. Shani Grimmond created a face using a plethora of pricey products, such as a $61 (£35) Marc Jacobs bronzer and a $69.50 (£39.50) Dior highlighter. For her cheaper look, she turned to more purse-friendly products like Maybelline and Rimmel, which cost under $17 (£10). Both beauty looks are strikingly similar in style, so can you tell which look is which?
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

            newsUS: {
                text: '@DailyMail',

              <script>
DM.later(['bundle', 'DOM_READY'], function() {
	var puffs, puff1, puff2,
		beta1, beta2,
	  	alpha1, alpha2,
	  	extra1, extra2;

	function debounce(func, wait, immediate) {
	    var timeout;
	    return function(evt) {
	      var context = this;
	      var args = arguments;
	      var later = function() {
	        timeout = null;
	        if (!immediate){
	          func.apply(context, args);
	        }
	      };
	      var callNow = immediate && !timeout;
	      clearTimeout(timeout);
	      timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
	      if (callNow){
	        func.apply(context, args);
	      }
	    };
	};

	var getExtra = function(a, b, p, d) {
  		var items = p.children(),
  			item, 
  			i, 
  			l = items.length,
  			h = 0,
  			extra = [];
  		d = Math.max(0, Math.max(0, d) + b.height() - a.height());
  		for(i = l; i-- && h < d;) {
  			item = $(items[i]);
  			if (item.hasClass('puff-ad') || item.hasClass('native-ad')) continue;
  			extra.push(item[0]);
  			h += item.height() + 5;
  			if (i == l - 1) item.children().removeClass('bottom');
  		}
  		return extra;
  	}

  	var process = function() {
  		console && console.time && console.time('puffs');

  		if (!puffs) {
	  		puffs = $('.beta .femail .puff ul, .beta .tvshowbiz .puff ul');
		  	puff1 = puffs[0] && $(puffs[0]);
		  	puff2 = puffs[1] && $(puffs[1]);
			beta1 = puff1 && puff1.parents('.beta');
		  	beta2 = puff2 && puff2.parents('.beta');
		  	alpha1 = beta1 && beta1.siblings('.alpha');
		  	alpha2 = beta2 && beta2.siblings('.alpha');
		}

	  	if (!puff1 || !beta1 || !alpha1) return;

  		extra1 = getExtra(alpha1, beta1, puff1, 0).reverse();
	  	DM.log && DM.log('puffs', 'puffs > extra1', extra1.length);

	  	if (alpha2 && beta2 && puff2) {
	  		$(extra1).prependTo(puff2);
                        extra2 = getExtra(alpha2, beta2, puff2, beta1.height() - alpha1.height());
	  		DM.log && DM.log('puffs', 'puffs > extra2', extra2.length);
	  		$(extra2).remove();
	  	} else {
	  		$(extra1).remove();
	  	}
	  	console && console.timeEnd && console.timeEnd('puffs');
	}

  	var fn = debounce(process, 500);
  	adsRenderer && adsRenderer.addLoadListener(function(ad) {
	    var id = !ad.isEmpty && ad.slot && ad.slot.molAd && ad.slot.molAd.parentId;
	    id && $('#' + id).parents('.beta')[0] && fn();
	}); 
	fn();
});
</script>

                <div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="51" />
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/femail/food/article-4487272/Frustrated-customers-share-photos-PizzaFails.html" >Another one bites the crust! Frustrated customers share photos of their #PizzaFails after their Italian treats were delivered without toppings or even the pie itself </a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/femail/food/article-4487272/Frustrated-customers-share-photos-PizzaFails.html">
                    <img  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/09/401F49E500000578-0-image-a-22_1494319777574.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Frustrated customers share photos of their #PizzaFails" />
                <noscript>
            
                <img  src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/09/401F49E500000578-0-image-a-22_1494319777574.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Frustrated customers share photos of their #PizzaFails" />
            
                </noscript>
            
        </a>
        <div >
        <p>
            
            Frustrated customers have taken to social media to share photos of their disastrous pizza deliveries with the hashtag #PizzaFails. In several photos customers were left shocked to discover that some of their toppings had been done away with completely including some pizzas served without cheese. But at least they were lucky enough to receive a whole pizza with one user sharing a photo with a bite taken from the pie and another box was found to be completely empty.
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

                <div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="61" />
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/sciencetech/article-4487700/Killer-whales-dining-great-white-shark-livers.html" >Are killer whales slaughtering great white sharks for their LIVERS? Orcas remove the organs with 'surgical precision' in a new spate of attacks</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/sciencetech/article-4487700/Killer-whales-dining-great-white-shark-livers.html">
                    <img  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/11/4020A67100000578-0-image-a-18_1494326283234.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Orcas dining on great white shark livers in South Africa" />
                <noscript>
            
                <img  src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/11/4020A67100000578-0-image-a-18_1494326283234.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Orcas dining on great white shark livers in South Africa" />
            
                </noscript>
            
        </a>
        <div >
        <p>
            
            At least three liver-less white shark carcasses have washed up near the popular tourist town Gansaabi, South Africa, so far in an unprecedented set of killings. Gansaabi is widely considered one of the best regions in the world for shark diving. Pictured are two of the carcasses found by local conservationists. Experts suggest that local killer whales have developed an appetite for squalene - an organic chemical compound found in abundance in shark liver oil.
        </p>
    </div>

    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview
     src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"

The video was captured by financial advisor Andrew Cohen who was visiting for a safari with his partner Candice. He said that while the elephant could have 'easily hurt' the buffalo it appeared that the enormous animal 'sensed that this was an innocent newborn and that it didn't mean any harm'.

                <div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="86" />
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-4488030/Heartbroken-monkey-clutches-child-collapsed.html" >Anguished mother's healing touch: Heartbroken monkey clutches her child after it collapsed... and it regains consciousness </a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-4488030/Heartbroken-monkey-clutches-child-collapsed.html">
                    <img  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/12/40204F2500000578-0-image-a-22_1494330937671.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Heartbroken monkey clutches her child after it collapsed" />
                <noscript>
            
                <img  src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/12/40204F2500000578-0-image-a-22_1494330937671.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Heartbroken monkey clutches her child after it collapsed" />
            
                </noscript>
            
        </a>
        <div >
        <p>
            
            The monkey, appearing to be wailing as it holds the limp body of her baby, was photographed in Jabalphur, India, by 31-year-old Avinash Lodhi. Happily moments after it was taken, the youngster appeared to make a full recovery.
        </p>

                <div class="article article-tri-headline">
  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a href="/femail/article-4487678/Hilarious-toddler-trying-vain-escape-SHADOW.html">Hilarious video captures frustrated toddler trying in vain to escape her own SHADOW by flapping her arms, stamping her feet and even turning upside down </a>
  </h2>
  <a href="/femail/article-4487678/Hilarious-toddler-trying-vain-escape-SHADOW.html">
    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview
     src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"
     data-src="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/2972077430135342601/636x382_JPG-SINGLE_2972077430135342601.jpg"
     width="636"
     height=382
     data-video="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/2972077430135342601/636x382_MP4_2972077430135342601.mp4"
     data-film="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/2972077430135342601/308x174_JPG_2972077430135342601.jpg"
     data-frame-width="308"
     data-frame-height="184"
     data-frame-count="43"
     data-fps="7"
     data-hd-film="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/2972077430135342601/636x382_JPG-HD_2972077430135342601.jpg"
     data-hd-frame-width="636"
     data-hd-frame-height="382"
     data-hd-frame-count="43"
     data-hd-fps="7" />

  </a>
  <div class="articletext">
    <div >
     <p>
       
       In the clip shared on YouTube the unnamed toddler from the US, enjoys a walk in the sunshine with her father but fails to grasp the concept of the shadow. She trials different positions in the hope to rid herself of her shadow while her dad can be heard laughing in the background. As she begins to walk again he asks 'did you get it off' to which she replies 'I can't' before bursting into tears. The adorable video has so far received more than 10,000 views on YouTube since its upload one day ago.
     </p>
    </div>

  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a itemprop="url" href="/travel/article-4477882/The-world-s-best-family-beach-breaks-2017-revealed.html">Free tropical stays for under-5s, a luxury Greek retreat with a creche and a chic Jamaican hotel where baby turtles hatch: The best family beach breaks revealed</a>
  </h2>
  <div class="articletext">

  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a href="/news/article-4487752/Labrador-ruins-cake-contest-scoffing-food.html">Greedy labrador ruins a dog cake-eating contest by wolfing down its own plate in seconds before scoffing everyone else’s </a>
  </h2>
  <a href="/news/article-4487752/Labrador-ruins-cake-contest-scoffing-food.html">
    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview
     src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"
     data-src="http://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2017/05/09/1154619889814226505/636x382_JPG-SINGLE_1154619889814226505.jpg"

     data-frame-count="26"

     data-hd-frame-width="636"
     data-hd-frame-height="382"
     data-hd-frame-count="26"
     data-hd-fps="7" />

  </a>
  <div class="articletext">
    <div >
     <p>
       
       The adorable pooch, pictured centre, scoffs all the food at once leaving nothing for the French bulldogs eagerly sat in front of their plates in the cute footage, which was recorded in an unknown location. The canine wolfs down the cake while dressed in a superman costume - with the two others at the side donning pumpkin and ghost outfits. The camera zooms in to show the disappointment on the face of one of the bulldogs after it realises there is nothing left to eat.
     </p>

                <div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="91" />
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/femail/article-4487764/Mother-transforms-frumpy-clothes-stylish-outfits.html" >Thrifty mother transforms frumpy clothes into stylish outfits for her two daughters (and even cut up a WEDDING DRESS)</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/femail/article-4487764/Mother-transforms-frumpy-clothes-stylish-outfits.html">
                    <img  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/12/4020C3A600000578-0-image-a-75_1494329503707.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Sarah Tyau transforms frumpy clothes into stylish outfits" />
                <noscript>
            
                <img  src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/09/12/4020C3A600000578-0-image-a-75_1494329503707.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Sarah Tyau transforms frumpy clothes into stylish outfits" />
            
                </noscript>
            
        </a>
        <div >
        <p>
            
            Sarah Tyau, 33, from Salt Lake City, Utah, has been transforming frumpy ensembles for her two daughters Adi, 9, and Ana, 8, the past six years. Her creations have now gained her more than 500,000 followers on Instagram. The talented designer would also like to progressively give greater percentages to charity - eventually seeing 100 per cent of proceeds going to children in need. Pictured: Sarah in an upcycled wedding dress (far left, and second from left) and Ana in a redesigned men's shirt (second from right and far right).
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

  </h2>
  <div class="articletext">

              <img  src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/05/08/19/40195A7F00000578-0-image-m-32_1494269903374.jpg" height="115" width="154" alt="" />

          </noscript>
      
    </a>
